   jQuery('.js__locale-selector__group').append('<li><a class="flag-all-other" id="js__flag__all-other" href="#">All Other</a>');

     =========
       _SLIDER.HTML OVERVIEW
 
       This file defines the featured products section for the category pages.
       If there are more products than what will fit on the screen, the slider
       overflows to the right and provides navigational arrows to the user.
       On mobile, it will become a simple side-swipe interface.
 
     =========
 
     =========
       USAGE
 
       This section is meant to be displayed in a full-width section.  It
       should support as many items as necessary, but the recommended number is
       less than 7.  It can handle as few as one product.
     =========
 
     -->

    <!--
 
     =========
       _SLIDER.HTML OVERVIEW
 
       This file defines the featured products section for the category pages.
       If there are more products than what will fit on the screen, the slider
       overflows to the right and provides navigational arrows to the user.
       On mobile, it will become a simple side-swipe interface.
 
     =========
 
     =========
       USAGE
 
       This section is meant to be displayed in a full-width section.  It
       should support as many items as necessary, but the recommended number is
       less than 7.  It can handle as few as one product.
     =========
 
     -->
    <h1 class="g__slider__header">
     Neue Produkte

     =========
       _HERO.HTML OVERVIEW

     =========
       _SLIDER.HTML OVERVIEW
 
       This file defines the featured products section for the category pages.
       If there are more products than what will fit on the screen, the slider
       overflows to the right and provides navigational arrows to the user.
       On mobile, it will become a simple side-swipe interface.
 
     =========
 
     =========
       USAGE
 
       This section is meant to be displayed in a full-width section.  It
       should support as many items as necessary, but the recommended number is
       less than 7.  It can handle as few as one product.
     =========
 
     -->
